# 오동나무 관 비용 제공 장례식장

전체 1,081개 장례식장 DB(`funeral_halls`) 스캔 결과.

## 검색 조건

`funeral_supplies` JSONB 배열 항목 중 다음 조건 모두 충족:

- `판매여부 = "Y"`
- `품종 = "관"`
- `품종상세 = "오동나무"` 또는 `품명`/`기타정보`에 "오동" 포함
- `요금 >= 10,000` (외부업체 위탁 표기 등 outlier 제외)

## 요약

| 구분 | 곳수 |
|---|---|
| 오동나무 관 가격 보유 | **955곳** |

## 평균 비용

### 장례식장별 최저가 기준 (관 종류 중 가장 저렴한 것)

| 구분 | 값 |
|---|---|
| 평균 | 219,127원 |
| 중간값 | 200,000원 |
| 최저 | 10,000원 |
| 최고 | 900,000원 |
| 표본 | 955곳 |

### 전체 오동나무 관 항목 기준

| 구분 | 값 |
|---|---|
| 평균 | 388,055원 |
| 중간값 | 350,000원 |
| 최저 | 10,000원 |
| 최고 | 3,500,000원 |
| 표본 | 4465건 |

> 💡 `funeral_supplies` 항목에는 시스템에서 산출한 `전국평균가격`(약 39만원) 필드도 포함되어 있음.

---

## 통계 집계 SQL (Postgres / Supabase)

`funeral_halls.funeral_supplies` JSONB 배열을 unnest해서 오동나무 관 항목만 집계.

### 장례식장별 최저가 + 전체 통계

```sql
WITH paulownia_coffin AS (
  SELECT
    h.facility_cd,
    h.company_name,
    item->>'품명'    AS item_name,
    (item->>'요금')::int AS amount
  FROM funeral_halls h
  CROSS JOIN LATERAL jsonb_array_elements(
    COALESCE(h.funeral_supplies, '[]'::jsonb)
  ) AS item
  WHERE item->>'판매여부' = 'Y'
    AND item->>'품종' = '관'
    AND (
      item->>'품종상세' = '오동나무'
      OR item->>'품명'    LIKE '%오동%'
      OR item->>'기타정보' LIKE '%오동%'
    )
    AND (item->>'요금')::int >= 10000
),
cheapest_per_hall AS (
  SELECT DISTINCT ON (facility_cd)
    facility_cd, company_name, item_name, amount
  FROM paulownia_coffin
  ORDER BY facility_cd, amount ASC
)
SELECT
  COUNT(*)::int                                              AS hall_count,
  ROUND(AVG(amount))::int                                    AS avg_cheapest,
  PERCENTILE_CONT(0.5) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY amount)::int   AS median_cheapest,
  MIN(amount)::int                                           AS min_cheapest,
  MAX(amount)::int                                           AS max_cheapest
FROM cheapest_per_hall;
```

기대 결과:
```
hall_count | avg_cheapest | median_cheapest | min_cheapest | max_cheapest
-----------+--------------+-----------------+--------------+-------------
       955 |       219127 |          200000 |        10000 |       900000
```

### Supabase RPC 함수

```sql
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION get_paulownia_stats()
RETURNS TABLE(
  hall_count int,
  avg_cheapest int,
  median_cheapest int,
  min_cheapest int,
  max_cheapest int
)
LANGUAGE sql STABLE AS 98999
  WITH paulownia_coffin AS (
    SELECT h.facility_cd, (item->>'요금')::int AS amount
    FROM funeral_halls h
    CROSS JOIN LATERAL jsonb_array_elements(
      COALESCE(h.funeral_supplies, '[]'::jsonb)
    ) AS item
    WHERE item->>'판매여부' = 'Y'
      AND item->>'품종' = '관'
      AND (
        item->>'품종상세' = '오동나무'
        OR item->>'품명'    LIKE '%오동%'
        OR item->>'기타정보' LIKE '%오동%'
      )
      AND (item->>'요금')::int >= 10000
  ),
  cheapest_per_hall AS (
    SELECT DISTINCT ON (facility_cd) facility_cd, amount
    FROM paulownia_coffin
    ORDER BY facility_cd, amount ASC
  )
  SELECT
    COUNT(*)::int,
    ROUND(AVG(amount))::int,
    PERCENTILE_CONT(0.5) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY amount)::int,
    MIN(amount)::int,
    MAX(amount)::int
  FROM cheapest_per_hall;
98999;
```

```ts
const { data } = await supabase.rpc('get_paulownia_stats');
const { hall_count, avg_cheapest } = data[0];
// `오동나무 관 비용 제공하는 ${hall_count}개 장례식장 평균 최저가 ${avg_cheapest.toLocaleString()}원`
```

### 장례식장별 최저가 리스트 (UI용)

```sql
SELECT DISTINCT ON (h.facility_cd)
  h.facility_cd,
  h.company_name,
  h.full_address,
  item->>'품명'        AS coffin_name,
  (item->>'요금')::int AS amount
FROM funeral_halls h
CROSS JOIN LATERAL jsonb_array_elements(
  COALESCE(h.funeral_supplies, '[]'::jsonb)
) AS item
WHERE item->>'판매여부' = 'Y'
  AND item->>'품종' = '관'
  AND (
    item->>'품종상세' = '오동나무'
    OR item->>'품명' LIKE '%오동%'
    OR item->>'기타정보' LIKE '%오동%'
  )
  AND (item->>'요금')::int >= 10000
ORDER BY h.facility_cd, (item->>'요금')::int ASC;
```
